Although you can go shopping downstairs, as the name suggests, the Sleepless City is very noisy and has many spotlights. Hotel guests on both sides may not be able to sleep until the noise is over. On the contrary The location of this hotel can be regarded as quiet in the bustle. Finally, the hardware in the room is good. From the wooden door handles, lights, nail sets, hair dryers, kettles, etc., the quality is guaranteed. The only thing I am not used to is that the toilet, shower room, and washbasin are all separate and cannot be closed. After the cleaning work is done on the assembly line, it would be a bit embarrassing if you are not living with an old couple or someone you know well üòÖ I am overall satisfied with the hotel!
